ArmyUnit/Description/Corpser=取得蜈蚣蠍的原質。蜈蚣蠍本身不重要，重要的是體內的寄生蟲。這組基因序能讓蟑螂把微型寄生蟲注入目標體內。酸性唾液溶解皮肉，寄生蟲鑽進宿主體內孕育，宿主一死，小蟑螂能自由從任何孔洞鑽出。非常有效。 /// Recovered scantipede essence. Scantipede itself unremarkable. Parasite within more interesting. Sequences allow roach to inject microscopic parasites. Acidic saliva melts away flesh. Allows parasite to burrow within host and gestate. Upon death, roachlings break free. Emerge from any available orifice. Extremely efficient.
ArmyUnit/Description/Hunter=獵殺蟲品系，戰略資源。利用極端條件來引導進化。獵殺蟲品系可以跳上山崖，出其不意攻擊敵人。牠們也能跳越蟲群部隊，轟炸敵人。毒爆蟲不會再被嗜血的異化蟲群給擋住去路。 /// Hunter strain, strategic asset. Extreme conditions used to guide evolution. Hunter strain can propel itself up cliffs, attack foes caught unawares. Able to leap over Swarm troops, bombard enemies. Banelings no longer trapped behind hungry zerglings.
ArmyUnit/Description/HydraliskImpaler=刺獸殖穴的原質在數千年前就已進化而成，依主宰的指示突變而成，是地刺殖穴的先祖品系。攻擊力強大。<n/><n/>將原質結合進刺蛇變形序列中，產生刺獸。只能攻擊單一目標，撕裂裝甲、血肉與骨骼。 /// Impaler colony essence evolved millennia ago. First mutated under Overmind's instruction. Ancestor strain of sunken colony. Powerful.<n/><n/>Can bond essence to hydralisk morph, create impaler. Attacks single foe. Tentacle shreds through armor, flesh, bone.
ArmyUnit/Description/HydraliskLurker=遁地獸品系在蟲群內戰之前就已完成。為了融入新品種，刀鋒女皇下令捨棄遁地獸原質。幾乎完全遺失，已成功回收，可以重組復原。<n/><n/>遁地獸遁地後，以脊刺同時攻擊複數敵人。對裝甲薄弱的敵人，有效。 /// Lurker evolved prior to inter-Swarm conflict. Essence abandoned by Queen of Blades in effort to assimilate new breeds. Almost lost. Now recovered. <n/><n/>Lurkers attack while burrowed. Spines strike multiple enemies at once. Effective against troops lacking sufficient armor.
ArmyUnit/Description/MutaliskBroodlord=寄生王蟲的變形基因幾乎消失，而腐化飛蟲品系數量銳減、無法取得原質，必須以飛螳彌補。<n/><n/>變形完成後，可孵化寄生蟲，從遠距離發射，自空中攻擊地面敵人。強大的武器。 /// Brood Lord strain almost lost. Corruptor strain unable to be reconstituted. Essence unavailable. Mutalisk base must suffice.<n/><n/>Once morphed, spawns broodling symbiotes. Able to launch broodlings long distance. Siege ground-based foes from air. Powerful weapon.
ArmyUnit/Description/MutaliskViper=飛蟒從澤瑞斯的原質演化而來。原生基因序，有效率。移除多餘突變。更強。適合蟲群。飛蟒品系能劫持目標，放出失能毒雲，讓蟲群獲得戰場優勢。 /// Viper adapted from essence taken on Zerus. Primal sequences streamlined. Redundant mutations removed. Stronger. Fit for Swarm. Viper strain abducts targets, emits disabling cloud. Manipulates battlefield conditions to Swarm's advantage.
ArmyUnit/Description/Noxious=自治聯盟的化合物，有意思。自治聯盟的科學家嘗試抑制蟲群的攻擊性，無意間創出強力毒素，對非蟲群的生物結構格外危險。沼獸品系的雷獸與毒素永久結合，可釋出劇毒氣體，並且透過甲殼內的導管來調節噴發毒素。 /// Dominion's compound, interesting. Scientists desired to pacify the Swarm, inadvertently created potent toxin. Deadly to any non-zerg entity. Noxious strain bonded permanently to toxins. Emits as poisonous vapor. Capable of channelling toxins and releasing in controlled blasts through vents in carapace.
ArmyUnit/Description/Raptor=吸收卡拉克的原質有許多好處：強化四頭肌、突變出蟲翅。結合這兩種因子，異化蟲可以飛躍空中，在山崖上下攀行，跳向遠處敵人。<n/><n/>輕微副作用：侵略性提高，導致攻擊力增加。可以接受該結果。 /// Assimilation of karak essence, many benefits. Can enhance quadriceps of zergling, mutate wing function. Would allow zergling to vault through air, climb up and down cliffs, leap at foes from distance.<n/><n/>Minor side effect: amplified aggression. Likely to improve damage output. Acceptable.
ArmyUnit/Description/Splitterling=分裂蟲品系具有分散式的神經系統，在攻城作戰中特別有效。分裂蟲爆炸時，屍體會分裂成兩隻小毒爆蟲繼續攻擊。只能分裂一次，繼續分裂只會變成不具思考能力的酸液。 /// Decentralized nervous system of splitter strain increases efficiency at siege warfare. Upon detonation, two baneling spawn split from remains, continue pressing assault. Split only occurs once. Further splits invariably result in acidic fluids of limited sentience.
ArmyUnit/Description/SwarmHostSplitA=可跟百生獸基因序成功結合的原質，稀有。原生蟲族基因架構可快速接受適應性，但自發變化的速度更快。食腐蟲巢的基因序可以讓卵囊產生永久突變，誕生飛行蝗蟲，跨越任意地形攻擊地面單位。 /// Essence capable of successfully bonding to swarm host sequences, uncommon. Primal framework accepts adaptations quickly, then overrides adaptations quicker. Carrion nest sequences allow permanent mutation of egg sac. Will birth flying locusts able to attack ground-based enemies across any terrain.
ArmyUnit/Description/SwarmHostSplitB=穿地獸品系以燼蟲原質加以強化。燼蟲分泌酵素來分解土壤、快速移動，進化後的百生獸品系能分泌蟲苔來達到類似的效果。深度挖掘可以讓穿地獸快速部署於覆有蟲苔的地點。 /// Creeper strain augmented by ash worm essence.
